</span><span id="L-1001"><a href="#L-1001"><span class="linenos">1001</span></a><span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">nicegui_page_sync_coro</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">dargs</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">**</span><span class="n">dkwargs</span><span class="p">):</span>
</span><span id="L-1002"><a href="#L-1002"><span class="linenos">1002</span></a><span class="w">    </span><span class="sd">&quot;&quot;&quot;Decorator. With an arguments. Gives ability to execute any decorated Cengal coroutine based page as a sync function.</span>
</span><span id="L-1003"><a href="#L-1003"><span class="linenos">1003</span></a><span class="sd">    Can postpone execution to the actual loop when possible if None as an immediate result (no result) is acceptible.</span>
</span><span id="L-1004"><a href="#L-1004"><span class="linenos">1004</span></a><span class="sd">    Can start own loop if needed. See sync_coro_param() decorator from cengal/parallel_execution/coroutines/coro_tools/wait_coro for more details</span>
</span><span id="L-1005"><a href="#L-1005"><span class="linenos">1005</span></a>

</span><span id="L-1263"><a href="#L-1263"><span class="linenos">1263</span></a><span class="c1"># # Async on_destroy handling is currently (08 Feb 2023) broken in NiceGUI: </span>

</span><span id="L-1273"><a href="#L-1273"><span class="linenos">1273</span></a><span class="c1"># Async on_destroy handling is currently (08 Feb 2023) broken in NiceGUI: </span>
</span><span id="L-1274"><a href="#L-1274"><span class="linenos">1274</span></a><span class="c1">#     they should await for handlers instead of current tasks creation approach</span>

With an arguments. Gives ability to execute any decorated Cengal coroutine based page as a sync function.</span>
</span><span id="nicegui_page_sync_coro-1004"><a href="#nicegui_page_sync_coro-1004"><span class="linenos">1004</span></a><span class="sd">    Can postpone execution to the actual loop when possible if None as an immediate result (no result) is acceptible.</span>
</span><span id="nicegui_page_sync_coro-1005"><a href="#nicegui_page_sync_coro-1005"><span class="linenos">1005</span></a><span class="sd">    Can start own loop if needed. See sync_coro_param() decorator from cengal/parallel_execution/coroutines/coro_tools/wait_coro for more details</span>

</span><span id="nicegui_page_sync_coro-1031"><a href="#nicegui_page_sync_coro-1031"><span class="linenos">1031</span></a>    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">nicegui_page_sync_coro_impl</span>
</span></pre></div>


            <div class="docstring"><p>Decorator. With an arguments. Gives ability to execute any decorated Cengal coroutine based page as a sync function.
Can postpone execution to the actual loop when possible if None as an immediate result (no result) is acceptible.
Can start own loop if needed. See sync_coro_param() decorator from cengal/parallel_execution/coroutines/coro_tools/wait_coro for more details</p>

<p>Returns:
    _type_: _description_</p>
</div>


                </section>

            <div class="docstring"><p>Decorator. With an arguments. Gives ability to execute any decorated Cengal coroutine based page as a sync function.
Can postpone execution to the actual loop when possible if None as an immediate result (no result) is acceptible.
Can start own loop if needed. See sync_coro_param() decorator from cengal/parallel_execution/coroutines/coro_tools/wait_coro for more details</p>

<p>Returns:
    _type_: _description_</p>
</div>


                </section>

            <div class="docstring"><p>Decorator. Without arguments. Makes a proper, fully functional async Page from any decorated Cengal coroutine</p>

    coro_worker (Worker): _description_</p>

<p>Raises:
    TypeError: _description_</p>

    _type_: _description_</p>

            <div class="docstring"><p>Prepares and starts NiceGUI. Saves initial args and kwargs parameters (as well as determined free port) into a tuple (Tuple[Tuple, Dict]) within an Instance service awailable by a 'cengal_nicegui__app_args_kwargs' string key </p>

<p>Args:
    host (str, optional): _description_. Defaults to '0.0.0.0'.
    port_or_range (Union[int, slice, Tuple[int, int]], optional): _description_. Defaults to 8080.
    title (str, optional): _description_. Defaults to 'NiceGUI'.
    viewport (str, optional): _description_. Defaults to 'width=device-width, initial-scale=1'.
    favicon (Optional[str], optional): _description_. Defaults to None.
    dark (Optional[bool], optional): _description_. Defaults to False.
    binding_refresh_interval (float, optional): _description_. Defaults to 0.1.
    show (bool, optional): _description_. Defaults to True.
    reload (bool, optional): _description_. Defaults to True.
    uvicorn_logging_level (str, optional): _description_. Defaults to 'warning'.
    uvicorn_reload_dirs (str, optional): _description_. Defaults to '.'.
    uvicorn_reload_includes (str, optional): _description_. Defaults to '<em>.py'.
    uvicorn_reload_excludes (str, optional): _description_. Defaults to '.</em>, .py[cod], .sw.<em>, ~</em>'.
    tailwind (bool, optional): _description_. Defaults to True.
    is_fast_loop (bool, optional): _description_. Defaults to True.
    main_coro (AnyWorker, optional): _description_. Defaults to None.</p>
</div>


                </section>
    </main>
